<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item
2.02&nbsp;Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On June&nbsp;28, 2006, the Registrant issued a press
release and held a conference call with analysts to report on the results of
operations for the second quarter of fiscal year 2006, which ended on May&nbsp;31,
2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furnished with this Form&nbsp;8-K as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1
is a copy of the press release labeled &#147;McCormick Reports Record Second Quarter
Results,&#148; which includes an unaudited Consolidated Income Statement for the
three and six month periods ended May&nbsp;31, 2006, an unaudited Consolidated
Balance Sheet of the Registrant as of May&nbsp;31, 2006, and an unaudited
Consolidated Statement of Cash Flows for the six months ended May&nbsp;31,
2006.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:12.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits.</font></u></p>

<p style="line-height:12.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&nbsp; Exhibits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The exhibit to this report is listed in Item 2.02
above and in the Exhibit&nbsp;Index that follows the signature line.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SIGNATURES</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, the Registrant has duly caused this report to be signed
on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">

<div>
 <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="604" height="93" src="g145251mai001.jpg"></font><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#160;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">FOR
IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;"><font style="text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK REPORTS&#160; RECORD SECOND QUARTER RESULTS</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">SPARKS, MD, JUNE 28 - - - McCormick &amp; Company, Incorporated
(NYSE:MKC), today reported results for the second quarter ended May 31, 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Success
with new products, marketing programs and pricing actions increased sales 2%
and in local currency 3%.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Gross
profit margin improved 0.8 percentage points to 39.2%.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Higher
sales and margins, as well as a gain on the sale of the Company&#146;s interest in a
joint venture led to earnings per share of 46&#162;, compared to 31&#162; in the prior
year.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">The
Company achieved these strong financial results while making excellent progress
on key initiatives to grow the business and improve profitability.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Second
quarter results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">In the second quarter, McCormick increased sales 2%, and in local
currency the increase was 3%.&#160; Success
with new products, marketing programs and pricing actions drove this
increase.&#160; During the quarter, the
reduction of low margin business reduced sales approximately 1%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">Gross profit margin reached 39.2%, a significant increase from 38.4% in
the prior year.&#160; Higher margin was driven
by pricing actions, efforts to lower costs and a more favorable business mix.&#160; In addition, gross profit margin in the
second quarter of 2005 was adversely affected by an operational accounting
adjustment related to a condiment operation in the U.K. In the second quarter
of 2006, cost of goods sold included $4 million of restructuring charges that
lowered gross profit margin 0.7 percentage points.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">Earnings per share rose to 46&#162; compared to 31&#162; in the second quarter of
2005.&#160; Increases in sales, gross profit
margin, interest income and income from unconsolidated operations, and lower
shares outstanding added 3&#162; to earnings per share. &#160;Stock-based compensation expense, which the
Company began to record in the first quarter of 2006, reduced earnings per
share 2&#162;. Actions related to the Company&#146;s restructuring program increased
earnings per share 14&#162;. One of these actions was a simplification of the
Company&#146;s joint venture structure that led to an after-tax gain of $27
million.&#160; During the second quarter,
McCormick acquired the remaining 49% interest in Dessert Products
International, S.A.S. (DPI) in exchange for its 50% interest in the Signature
Brands, LLC joint venture. Restructuring </font></p>


 <p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman">1</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\fc\179882171_D11744_1196339\14525-1-ma.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jun 28 08:08 2006' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
 <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"></p>


<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">charges
related to facility closures and a voluntary separation program offset a
portion of the gain during the second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial outlook</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">The gain on the
joint venture transaction increased earnings per share 20&#162; and led to an
increase in the Company&#146;s projected earnings per share for 2006 to $1.41-$1.44
from $1.21-$1.24.&#160; This transaction also
affected certain financial projections related to McCormick&#146;s restructuring
program. Including the gain and the latest projections, pre-tax charges for the
program are expected to range from $110-$130 million compared to the initial
estimate of $130-$150 million. Despite the reduction in charges, expected
annual cost savings remain at $50 million. The projection for the cash portion
of the charges continues to be $85-$100 million, of which approximately $60
million is expected to be spent in 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">On June 27, 2006
the Company completed the acquisition of the assets of Epicurean International.
This business develops, imports and markets the <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Thai
Kitchen&#174;</font></i> and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Simply Asia&#174;</font></i>
brands and has annual sales of approximately $50 million. Acquisitions are part
of the Company&#146;s growth strategy and an important driver of its goals to grow
sales 3-5% and increase earnings per share 8-10%. This earnings per share goal
excludes charges related to the restructuring program and in 2006, stock-based
compensation expense. In 2006, the charges related to the restructuring program
are expected to reduce earnings per share 22&#162;, although this projection could
be affected by the timing of the various actions related to the program.
Stock-based compensation expense is expected to reduce earnings per share by
11&#162; in 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Chairman&#146;s
comments</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">Robert J. Lawless, Chairman, President &amp; CEO, commented, &#147;We have
had strong financial results through the first half of our 2006 fiscal year. Despite
the elimination of some low margin business, sales in local currency were up
3%. Both the consumer and industrial businesses are benefiting from the launch
of new products, cost savings programs and pricing actions that provide an
offset to the higher costs of packaging, energy and benefits. We have increased
gross profit margin 1.1 percentage points, including a 0.4 percentage point
reduction due to restructuring charges. The Company is on track with its 2006
goal to increase gross profit margin 1.0 percentage point. Our joint venture in
Mexico has had a strong six month performance and our share repurchases have
further increased earnings per share. An excellent first half performance
provides us with the opportunity to finish the year at the upper end of our
projected earnings per share range while continuing our investment in
advertising, promotion and other growth initiatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#147;We continue to make good progress on several key initiatives.&#160; First is our initiative to grow through
acquisitions. Yesterday we completed an acquisition that provides a point of
entry into the Asian food category.&#160; The <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Thai Kitchen&#174;</font></i> and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Simply Asia&#174;</font></i>
brands provide authentic, easy-to-prepare Asian foods to North American
consumers. Sales of these brands are growing rapidly and since 2002 have
achieved a 32% compound annual growth rate. This business fits squarely with
our strategy to acquire specialty and ethnic food businesses that complement
our established leadership in the development and marketing of flavors for
food.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#147;Second, the revitalization of our spice and seasoning products in the
U.S. is now underway. Our products now feature new labels with contemporary
graphics, a more consistent appearance and attractive food photography. We are
adding new products such as roasting rubs, signature blends and gourmet
grinders. In August, we will begin to replace our current shelves with a new
gravity-feed merchandising system in certain markets, and in the fourth </font></p>


 <p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\fc\179882171_D11744_1196339\14525-1-ma.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jun 28 08:08 2006' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
 <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"></p>


<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">quarter
will convert to new flip-top caps for our bottles.&#160; Based on the consumer and retailer response
to test markets, we are excited about the potential to gain consumer attention
and increased demand as this initiative unfolds over the next three years.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#147;Third, a number of actions have been taken to transform our U.S.
industrial business. As we focus our attention and resources on our strategic
customers, we have gained access to previously untapped opportunities to
develop new products and have more insight into these customers&#146; forecasts. In
order to reduce complexity and improve margins, we embarked on a plan to end
our relationship with smaller customers that contribute marginally to sales and
have no significant profit impact. We have already met our goal to reduce the
number of customers by 25% and are likely to exceed this initial target. Another
round of price increases was put into effect June 1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:7.0pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">st</font><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#160;that bring
product margins to target thresholds.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#147;Fourth, we continue to move forward with our broad restructuring
program. Dedicated teams are working on previously announced facility
consolidations and we are lowering costs with a voluntary separation program in
the U.S. In fact, the closure of our second largest manufacturing facility
worldwide is ahead of schedule at this time. An important step in simplifying
the business was completed in May with the streamlining of our joint venture
structure. This led to our ownership of 100% of DPI and the Vahine business,
which is the leading brand of dessert aids in Europe.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#147;These are important initiatives that are well-planned and are being
well-executed. Our leadership team and employees throughout McCormick are
working hard and making great progress. As we position the Company for the
future, I am confident that McCormick&#146;s shareholders can look forward to
increased sales, improved margins and higher profits.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Business Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-style:italic;">In the
first quarter of 2006, the Company made several changes to the way it reports
its business segment results.&#160; These
changes are described following the financial results for the consumer and
industrial businesses.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  </td>
  <td width="0%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:.34%;">
  <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>

 <tr height="0">
  <td width="443" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="18" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="8" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="50" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="18" style="border:none;"></td>

  <td width="50" style="border:none;"></td>

  <td width="50" style="border:none;"></td>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-style:italic;">*&#160;
The Company began recording stock-based compensation expense in the
first quarter of 2006.&#160; Stock
compensation expense recorded in the consumer business operating results was
$3.1 million in the second quarter and $8.9 million year-to-date.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">For the second quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer business rose 2%
compared to the prior year and in local currency increased 3%. This increase
was driven largely by pricing actions, new product sales and marketing programs
that increased base business sales. The elimination of low margin business reduced
sales approximately 1%. Sales in the Americas rose 6% and in local currency 5%
as a result of pricing, new products and an increase in base business sales.
Consumer sales in Europe declined 7%, and in local currency declined 2%. A </font></p>


 <p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman">3</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\fc\179882171_D11744_1196339\14525-1-ma.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jun 28 08:08 2006' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
 <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"></p>


<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">portion
of the decrease related to the Company&#146;s decision to exit its business in
Finland, as well as the timing of customer purchases that occurred in the first
quarter, in advance of the implementation of B2K. In the Asia/Pacific region
the Company eliminated a low margin co-packing business that led to a second
quarter sales decline of 1% and an increase of 1% in local currency.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">For the consumer business, operating income excluding restructuring
charges in the second quarter of 2006 was $48.8 million compared to $53.4 million
in 2005. The decrease was due to $3.1 million of stock-based compensation
expense, as well as increases in advertising expense, incentive compensation
and costs associated with the implementation of B2K in Europe. In the second
quarter of 2006, higher sales and operating income for the consumer business in
the Americas, offset a portion of these expense increases. In addition, the
second quarter of 2005 included the impact of an operational accounting
adjustment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-style:italic;">*&#160;
The Company began recording stock-based compensation expense in the
first quarter of 2006.&#160; Stock
compensation expense recorded in the industrial business operating results was
$1.8 million in the second quarter and $4.8 million year-to-date.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">For the second quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business
increased 2% compared to the prior year. The increase was driven primarily by
higher volume related to new product introductions by the Company&#146;s U.S.
customers. The elimination of low margin business reduced sales approximately
1%. New products drove sales in the Americas, which were up 5% and in local
currency rose 4%.&#160; In Europe, sales
declined 6% and in local currency declined 1%. Sales in the Asia/Pacific region
decreased 8% and in local currency decreased 9%. In both of these regions, the
Company eliminated certain low margin items, which reduced sales, but had minimal
profit impact. Actions to reduce customers and products in North America will
reduce sales and to a lesser extent profits, beginning in the third quarter of
2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">For
the industrial business, operating income excluding restructuring charges rose
$1.8 million, including $1.8 million of stock-based compensation expense. Operating
income in the second quarter of 2006 was driven by higher sales and
significantly improved gross profit margin. In addition, the second quarter of
2005 included the impact of an operational accounting adjustment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Changes
in Reporting Business Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">In the first quarter of 2006, the Company changed the way it internally
reports its business segment results. In line with this change, the segment
results above have also been changed and prior periods have been restated to be
comparable.&#160; The changes are summarized
below:</font></p>


 <p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman">4</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\fc\179882171_D11744_1196339\14525-1-ma.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jun 28 08:08 2006' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
 <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"></p>


<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;">Operating income internally
is measured by management excluding restructuring charges. The information
provided above displays operating income for each segment with and without
restructuring charges. As noted below, management believes this information is
relevant to analyze business performance and trends.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;">The Company decided to
allocate 100% of its selling, general and administrative expenses to the
business segments beginning in the first quarter of 2006. The Company believes
that this more complete allocation better represents the profitability of its
two segments.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:11.0pt;">The sales and income related
to warehouse club customers are now managed in the consumer business.&#160; Through 2005, this was managed in the
industrial business.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">The Company has posted to its website, restated historical business
segment results for each quarter of 2005 at ir.mccormick.com under the heading
&#147;Financial Information&#148; and &#147;2005 Business Segment Restatement.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">In addition to the changes noted above, the Company also adopted SFAS
123R. This has a significant effect on each of the business segments and
accordingly, the effect is noted with the segment financial results reported
above.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">The pro forma information excluding
restructuring charges in this press release are not measures that are defined
in generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;). These items are measures
that management believe are important to adjust for in order to have a
meaningful comparison to prior and future periods and to provide a basis for
future projections and for estimating our earnings growth prospects. These
non-GAAP measures are used by management as a performance measure to judge
profitability of our business absent the restructuring related items. Management
also analyzes its business performance and trends excluding amounts related to
restructuring. These measures provide a more consistent view of performance
than the closest GAAP equivalent for management and investors. Management
compensates for this by using these measures in combination with the GAAP
measures. The presentation of the non-GAAP measures in this press release are
made alongside the most directly comparable GAAP measures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pro forma Information</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">The Company has provided below certain pro forma financial results
excluding amounts related to streamlining actions in 2005 and a restructuring
program in 2006. In addition, the impact of stock-based compensation expense,
which the Company began to record as &#147;Selling, general and administrative
expense&#148; in the first quarter of 2006, is noted.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 10.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">No
stock-based compensation expense was recorded in 2005. In the second quarter of
2006, stock-based compensation expense of $5.0 million had an after-tax impact
of $3.4 million. For the first six months of 2006, stock-based compensation
expense of $13.7 million had an after-tax impact of $9.3 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">No stock-based compensation
expense was recorded in 2005. In the second quarter of 2006, stock-based
compensation expense reduced earnings per share by $0.02. For the first six months
of 2006, stock-based compensation expense reduced earnings per share by $0.07.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">As previously announced, McCormick will hold a conference call with analysts
today at 10:00 a.m. ET. The conference call will be web cast live via the
McCormick web site. Go to ir.mccormick.com and follow directions to listen to
the call and access the accompanying presentation materials. At this same
location, a replay of the call will be available following the live call. Past
press releases and additional information can be found at this address.</font></p>

current views and assumptions and involve risks and uncertainties that could be

customer relationships, ability to realize expected cost savings and margin

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About McCormick</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">McCormick &amp; Company, Incorporated is the global leader in the
manufacture, marketing and distribution of spices, seasonings and flavors to
the entire food industry &#150; to foodservice and food manufacturers as well as to
retail outlets.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

information contact:</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">Corporate Communications: John
McCormick (410-771-7110 or john_mccormick@mccormick.com)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">Investor Relations: Joyce
